CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS r0932517_kookclub;

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.gemeente ( 
	postcode             char(4)  NOT NULL  ,
	gemeente             varchar(30)  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_gemeente_postcode PRIMARY KEY ( postcode )
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.gerecht ( 
	naam                 varchar(60)  NOT NULL  ,
	beschrijving         varchar(100)  NOT NULL  ,
	bereidtijd           smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_gerecht_naam PRIMARY KEY ( naam )
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.ingrediënt ( 
	naam                 varchar(30)  NOT NULL  ,
	eenheid              varchar(20)  NOT NULL  ,
	energie              integer  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_ingredient_naam PRIMARY KEY ( naam )
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.ingrediënt_in_gerecht ( 
	gerecht              varchar(60)  NOT NULL  ,
	ingrediënt           varchar(30)  NOT NULL  ,
	hoeveelheid          integer  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_ingredient_in_gerecht PRIMARY KEY ( ingrediënt, gerecht ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_ingredient_in_gerecht_gerecht FOREIGN KEY ( gerecht ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.gerecht( naam )   ,
	CONSTRAINT fk_ingredient_in_gerecht_ingredient FOREIGN KEY ( ingrediënt ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.ingrediënt( naam )   
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.lid ( 
	lidnr                integer  NOT NULL  ,
	naam                 varchar(35)  NOT NULL  ,
	voornaam             varchar(30)  NOT NULL  ,
	geboortedatum        date  NOT NULL  ,
	geslacht             char(1)    ,
	postcode             char(4)  NOT NULL  ,
	straat               varchar(40)  NOT NULL  ,
	huisnr               smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	gsmnr                char(10)    ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_lid_lidnr PRIMARY KEY ( lidnr ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_lid_gemeente FOREIGN KEY ( postcode ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.gemeente( postcode )   
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.thema ( 
	naam                 varchar(25)  NOT NULL  ,
	beschrijving         varchar(50)  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_thema_naam PRIMARY KEY ( naam )
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.gerecht_past_in_thema ( 
	gerecht              varchar(60)  NOT NULL  ,
	thema                varchar(25)  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_gerecht_past_in_thema PRIMARY KEY ( gerecht, thema ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_gerecht_past_in_thema_gerecht FOREIGN KEY ( gerecht ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.gerecht( naam )   ,
	CONSTRAINT fk_gerecht_past_in_thema_thema FOREIGN KEY ( thema ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.thema( naam )   
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.kookworkshop ( 
	workshop_id          smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	startmoment          timestamp(0)  NOT NULL  ,
	duur                 smallint    ,
	max_deelnemers       smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	thema                varchar(25)  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_kookworkshop_workshop_id PRIMARY KEY ( workshop_id ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_kookworkshop_thema FOREIGN KEY ( thema ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.thema( naam )   
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.deelname ( 
	lid                  integer  NOT NULL  ,
	workshop             smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	inschrijfdatum       timestamp(0)  NOT NULL  ,
	score                smallint    ,
	feedback             varchar(100)    ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_deelname PRIMARY KEY ( lid, workshop ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_deelname_kookworkshop FOREIGN KEY ( workshop ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.kookworkshop( workshop_id )   ,
	CONSTRAINT fk_deelname_lid FOREIGN KEY ( lid ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.lid( lidnr )   
 );

CREATE  TABLE r0932517_kookclub.gerecht_in_workshop ( 
	workshop             smallint  NOT NULL  ,
	gerecht              varchar(60)  NOT NULL  ,
	rol_in_menu          varchar(20)  NOT NULL  ,
	CONSTRAINT pk_gerecht_in_workshop PRIMARY KEY ( workshop, gerecht ),
	CONSTRAINT fk_gerecht_in_workshop_gerecht FOREIGN KEY ( gerecht ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.gerecht( naam )   ,
	CONSTRAINT fk_gerecht_in_workshop_kookworkshop FOREIGN KEY ( workshop ) REFERENCES r0932517_kookclub.kookworkshop( workshop_id )   
 );
